[2026-03-04T07:11:06Z] Akshay: The X theory is an analogy coined by the political scientist Walter Russell Mead to explain the myriad theories and explanations offered for the US Israel relationship. It is a reference to the astronomer/mathematician Urbain Le Verrier, who was the first to observe a slight precession in the orbit of Y, which he hypothesized was due to the existence of a planet, which he named X. In doing so Le Verrier was applying the same logic he had used to discover the planet Z based on the observed squiggles in the orbit of A. This proved to be fallacious however, and the precession of X was later explained using B’s seminal theory. ID X Y Z A B

[2026-03-04T16:02:28Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: 5.	Mandaeism is an ancient Gnostic religion, possibly the last surviving form of Gnosticism. It venerates Adam as a prophet and regards “X the Y” (known to them as yAhyA) as the greatest and final prophet, while explicitly rejecting Jesus, Abraham, and Moses. Their most important ritual is “masbuta,” a form of Y performed in flowing water. In Christian tradition, “X the Y” is recognized as a prophet who performed Y on Jesus of Nazareth. According to the Gospel of Luke, “X the Y” and Jesus are relatives. ID X and Y.

[2026-03-04T16:09:05Z] Pavan Pamidimarri: 6.	X was born in 1805 in Sharon, Vermont. At the age of 14, confused by the competing claims of local Protestant denominations, he reportedly went into a grove of trees to pray and experienced what his followers call the "First Vision." He later claimed that an angel named Moroni directed him to a hill called Cumorah, where he unearthed a set of golden plates inscribed in "reformed Egyptian." He said he translated them using two seer stones called the Urim and Thummim. The resulting book was first published in Palmyra, New York, in 1830 — the same year he formally organized his Y church with six members. He was killed by a mob in Carthage, Illinois, in 1844. ID X and Y.

This secretive monotheistic religion originated in the 11th century in Egypt, during the reign of the Fatimid Caliph al-Hakim bi-Amr Allah, whom followers regard as a divine manifestation. [2026-03-04T17:34:12Z] Abhishek Vats: Q. It is a common misconception that all Xs fall over when they are excited, but the phenomenon is actually specific to a single breed: the Myotonic X, more popularly known as the "Fainting X." ↵ The "fainting" isn't actually a loss of consciousness or a result of being tired; it is a hereditary genetic condition called myotonia congenita. Because the muscles stiffen so suddenly, the X loses its balance. If the X is standing still, it might just stiffen like a board and tip over sideways. If it is running when the "faint" occurs, its legs lock up, and momentum causes it to tumble. Id X
